let update: (Model, Action) -> Model =
  fun (buffer, todos) ->
    case todos
    | AddTodo => (buffer, add(todos, buffer $== "" 
                          && [ (buffer, true) ] ) )
    | RemoveTodo(index) => remove(index, todos)
    | ToggleTodo(index) => toggle(index, todos)
    | UpdateBuffer(buffer) => (buffer, todos) end in
